# English Core 3000

NGSL 1.2 + NGSL supplementary + NAWL fill. Ranked by frequency.

## 1. the

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; art.
- IPA (UK): /ðə/
- Chinese: 这；那（定冠词）
- Collocation: the same;the first;the more
- Example: The book on the table is mine.
- 例句: 桌上的那本书是我的。
- MemoryTip: 元音前常读 /ðiː/，辅音前读 /ðə/。

## 2. be

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /biː/
- Chinese: 是；在；成为
- Collocation: be careful;be honest;there be
- Example: She wants to be a doctor one day.
- 例句: 她希望有一天成为医生。
- Synonym: exist;remain
- MemoryTip: am/is/are/was/were 都是 be 的词形。

## 3. and

- CEFR: A1
- POS: conj.
- IPA (UK): /ænd/
- Chinese: 和；并且
- Collocation: and so on;bread and butter;and then
- Example: Tom and Lily walked home together.
- 例句: 汤姆和莉莉一起走回家。
- Synonym: plus;also
- Antonym: but;or
- MemoryTip: 连接对等成分，可记成“一加一”。

## 4. of

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.
- IPA (UK): /əv/
- Chinese: ……的；属于
- Collocation: a lot of;kind of;proud of
- Example: This is a photo of my family.
- 例句: 这是我家的一张照片。
- Synonym: from;about
- MemoryTip: 弱读常见 /əv/，别总读成 /ɒv/。

## 5. to

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; particle
- IPA (UK): /tuː/
- Chinese: 到；向；去；不定式标记
- Collocation: go to;listen to;want to
- Example: I need to finish my homework tonight.
- 例句: 我今晚需要完成作业。
- Synonym: towards;for
- Antonym: from
- MemoryTip: 作不定式时多弱读 /tə/。

## 6. a

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; art.
- IPA (UK): /ə/
- Chinese: 一个（不定冠词）
- Collocation: a bit;a few;have a look
- Example: She bought a gift for her friend.
- 例句: 她给朋友买了一份礼物。
- Synonym: one;any
- Antonym: the
- MemoryTip: 辅音前用 a，元音前改用 an。

## 7. in

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /ɪn/
- Chinese: 在……里；在……时
- Collocation: in time;in fact;in the morning
- Example: There are three books in the bag.
- 例句: 包里有三本书。
- Synonym: inside;within
- Antonym: out;outside
- MemoryTip: in 像走进门里。

## 8. have

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /hæv/
- Chinese: 有；吃；经历；助动词
- Collocation: have lunch;have to;have fun
- Example: They have a small flat near the station.
- 例句: 他们在车站附近有一套小公寓。
- Synonym: own;possess
- Antonym: lack
- MemoryTip: 完成时里 have/has + 过去分词。

## 9. it

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.
- IPA (UK): /ɪt/
- Chinese: 它；这；形式主语
- Collocation: it seems;find it;make it
- Example: It is raining hard this afternoon.
- 例句: 今天下午雨下得很大。
- Synonym: this;that
- MemoryTip: 指物、动物、时间天气常用 it。

## 10. you

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.
- IPA (UK): /juː/
- Chinese: 你；你们
- Collocation: thank you;see you;you know
- Example: Can you help me with this box?
- 例句: 你能帮我搬这个箱子吗？
- Synonym: one;people
- MemoryTip: 单复数同形，语气看语境。

## 11. he

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.
- IPA (UK): /hiː/
- Chinese: 他
- Collocation: he says;he is;there he is
- Example: He is waiting for the bus outside.
- 例句: 他在外面等公交车。
- Antonym: she
- MemoryTip: 主格 he，宾格 him，所有格 his。

## 12. for

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; conj.
- IPA (UK): /fɔː(r)/
- Chinese: 为了；给；因为；达……之久
- Collocation: for example;look for;wait for
- Example: This gift is for your sister.
- 例句: 这份礼物是给你妹妹的。
- Synonym: because of;during
- Antonym: against
- MemoryTip: 表目的、对象或时间长度都很常见。

## 13. they

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.
- IPA (UK): /ðeɪ/
- Chinese: 他们；她们；它们
- Collocation: they say;there they are;as they
- Example: They arrived early for the meeting.
- 例句: 他们早早到了会议现场。
- Synonym: people
- MemoryTip: 主格 they，宾格 them，所有格 their。

## 14. not

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; particle
- IPA (UK): /nɒt/
- Chinese: 不；没有
- Collocation: not only;do not;not yet
- Example: I do not want to go out tonight.
- 例句: 我今晚不想出门。
- Synonym: no;never
- Antonym: yes
- MemoryTip: 常缩成 n't，如 don't / isn't。

## 15. that

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.; conj.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /ðæt/
- Chinese: 那个；那；引导从句
- Collocation: so that;that day;find that
- Example: I think that the answer is correct.
- 例句: 我认为这个答案是正确的。
- Synonym: which;this
- Antonym: this
- MemoryTip: 可指物，也可引导 that 从句。

## 16. we

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.
- IPA (UK): /wiː/
- Chinese: 我们
- Collocation: we are;as we;shall we
- Example: We are planning a trip next month.
- 例句: 我们计划下个月去旅行。
- Synonym: us
- MemoryTip: 主格 we，宾格 us，所有格 our。

## 17. on

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /ɒn/
- Chinese: 在……上；关于；继续
- Collocation: on time;on the table;turn on
- Example: The keys are on the kitchen table.
- 例句: 钥匙在厨房桌上。
- Synonym: upon;about
- Antonym: off;under
- MemoryTip: 接触表面用 on，反义常想 off。

## 18. with

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.
- IPA (UK): /wɪð/
- Chinese: 和……一起；用；带有
- Collocation: with care;deal with;along with
- Example: She went to the cinema with her friends.
- 例句: 她和朋友们一起去看电影了。
- Synonym: alongside;using
- Antonym: without
- MemoryTip: with 的反义是 without。

## 19. this

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /ðɪs/
- Chinese: 这；这个
- Collocation: this morning;this way;like this
- Example: This café makes excellent coffee.
- 例句: 这家咖啡馆咖啡很好。
- Synonym: these;that
- Antonym: that
- MemoryTip: 近处 this，远处 that；复数 these。

## 20. i

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.
- IPA (UK): /aɪ/
- Chinese: 我
- Collocation: I think;I am;I hope
- Example: I usually get up at seven.
- 例句: 我通常七点起床。
- Synonym: me
- MemoryTip: 句子开头须大写 I。

## 21. do

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; aux.
- IPA (UK): /duː/
- Chinese: 做；干；助动词
- Collocation: do homework;do well;how do you
- Example: What do you usually do at weekends?
- 例句: 你周末通常做什么？
- Synonym: perform;act
- MemoryTip: 疑问/否定句里常用 do/does/did。

## 22. as

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; conj.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /æz/
- Chinese: 作为；当……时；像；因为
- Collocation: as well;as soon as;as for
- Example: She works as a nurse in hospital.
- 例句: 她在医院当护士。
- Synonym: like;while
- MemoryTip: as…as 表示同等比较。

## 23. at

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.
- IPA (UK): /æt/
- Chinese: 在（地点/时间点）；朝向
- Collocation: at home;at least;look at
- Example: We will meet at the station at six.
- 例句: 我们六点在车站见面。
- Synonym: in;on
- MemoryTip: 具体时刻、较小地点常用 at。

## 24. she

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.
- IPA (UK): /ʃiː/
- Chinese: 她
- Collocation: she says;she is;there she is
- Example: She teaches English at our school.
- 例句: 她在我们学校教英语。
- Antonym: he
- MemoryTip: 主格 she，宾格 her，所有格 her。

## 25. but

- CEFR: A1
- POS: conj.; prep.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /bʌt/
- Chinese: 但是；除了
- Collocation: but also;nothing but;last but not least
- Example: I like tea, but I prefer coffee.
- 例句: 我喜欢茶，但更爱咖啡。
- Synonym: however;yet
- Antonym: and
- MemoryTip: 转折用 but，语气比 however 更口语。

## 26. from

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.
- IPA (UK): /frɒm/
- Chinese: 从；来自；由于
- Collocation: from home;far from;different from
- Example: This letter is from my uncle in London.
- 例句: 这封信来自我在伦敦的叔叔。
- Synonym: out of;since
- Antonym: to;towards
- MemoryTip: from A to B：从 A 到 B。

## 27. by

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /baɪ/
- Chinese: 被；通过；在旁边；到……之前
- Collocation: by bus;by chance;by the way
- Example: The report was written by my colleague.
- 例句: 这份报告是我同事写的。
- Synonym: via;near
- MemoryTip: 被动语态里 by 引出动作执行者。

## 28. will

- CEFR: A1
- POS: modal; noun
- IPA (UK): /wɪl/
- Chinese: 将；会；意愿；遗嘱
- Collocation: will be;free will;if you will
- Example: They will call you tomorrow morning.
- 例句: 他们明天早上会给你打电话。
- Synonym: shall;going to
- Antonym: won't
- MemoryTip: 表将来也表意愿；won't = will not。

## 29. or

- CEFR: A1
- POS: conj.
- IPA (UK): /ɔː(r)/
- Chinese: 或者；否则
- Collocation: or so;either or;or else
- Example: Would you like tea or coffee?
- 例句: 你想喝茶还是咖啡？
- Synonym: alternatively
- Antonym: and
- MemoryTip: either…or… 表示二选一。

## 30. say

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /seɪ/
- Chinese: 说；表示
- Collocation: say hello;say sorry;that is to say
- Example: Please say your name clearly.
- 例句: 请清楚地说出你的名字。
- Synonym: speak;tell;state
- Antonym: listen
- MemoryTip: say 侧重说的内容；tell 常带对象。

## 31. go

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /ɡəʊ/
- Chinese: 去；走；变得
- Collocation: go home;go on;go shopping
- Example: We usually go to school by bike.
- 例句: 我们通常骑自行车去上学。
- Synonym: leave;travel;move
- Antonym: stay;come
- MemoryTip: go + -ing：go swimming / go shopping。

## 32. so

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; conj.
- IPA (UK): /səʊ/
- Chinese: 如此；所以；这样
- Collocation: so that;so far;and so on
- Example: It was raining, so we stayed inside.
- 例句: 下雨了，所以我们待在屋里。
- Synonym: therefore;very
- MemoryTip: 既表程度（so tired），也表结果。

## 33. all

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /ɔːl/
- Chinese: 全部；所有；完全
- Collocation: all day;above all;all over
- Example: All students must wear school uniforms.
- 例句: 所有学生都必须穿校服。
- Synonym: every;entire
- Antonym: none;some
- MemoryTip: all of us = 我们全部。

## 34. if

- CEFR: A1
- POS: conj.
- IPA (UK): /ɪf/
- Chinese: 如果；是否
- Collocation: if possible;what if;as if
- Example: If it rains, we will cancel the trip.
- 例句: 如果下雨，我们就取消这次旅行。
- Synonym: whether;when
- MemoryTip: 真实条件用 will；虚拟则改时态。

## 35. one

- CEFR: A1
- POS: num.; pron.; det.
- IPA (UK): /wʌn/
- Chinese: 一；一个人；某一个
- Collocation: one day;one of;the one
- Example: One of my friends lives abroad.
- 例句: 我的一个朋友住在国外。
- Synonym: a;single
- Antonym: many;none
- MemoryTip: 可替代前文名词：this one / that one。

## 36. would

- CEFR: A1
- POS: modal
- IPA (UK): /wʊd/
- Chinese: 会；愿意；过去将来
- Collocation: would like;would rather;would you
- Example: I would like a glass of water, please.
- 例句: 请给我一杯水。
- Synonym: could;might
- MemoryTip: would like = want 的更礼貌说法。

## 37. about

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /əˈbaʊt/
- Chinese: 关于；大约；到处
- Collocation: talk about;about time;think about
- Example: We talked about our weekend plans after lunch.
- 例句: 午饭后我们聊了周末的计划。
- Synonym: regarding;around
- Antonym: exactly
- MemoryTip: about 可记成绕着一件事转。

## 38. can

- CEFR: A1
- POS: modal; noun
- IPA (UK): /kæn/
- Chinese: 能；可以；罐头
- Collocation: can do;as you can;can of
- Example: Can you open the window, please?
- 例句: 请你把窗户打开好吗？
- Synonym: could;may;able to
- Antonym: cannot
- MemoryTip: 否定 can't；过去/委婉用 could。

## 39. which

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.; det.
- IPA (UK): /wɪtʃ/
- Chinese: 哪一个；……的（关系代词）
- Collocation: which one;in which;of which
- Example: Which colour do you prefer?
- 例句: 你更喜欢哪种颜色？
- Synonym: that;what
- MemoryTip: 问选择用 which；非限定从句也常用。

## 40. there

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; pron.
- IPA (UK): /ðeə(r)/
- Chinese: 在那里；有（there be）
- Collocation: over there;there is;out there
- Example: There is a park near my house.
- 例句: 我家附近有一座公园。
- Synonym: here
- Antonym: here
- MemoryTip: there be 表“存在”，非地点时也可用。

## 41. know

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /nəʊ/
- Chinese: 知道；认识；了解
- Collocation: know about;get to know;as you know
- Example: Do you know the way to the museum?
- 例句: 你知道去博物馆怎么走吗？
- Synonym: understand;recognise
- Antonym: ignore
- MemoryTip: know that… = 知道某事属实。

## 42. more

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; adv.; pron.
- IPA (UK): /mɔː(r)/
- Chinese: 更多；更加
- Collocation: more than;once more;more or less
- Example: I need more time to finish this task.
- 例句: 我需要更多时间完成这项任务。
- Synonym: additional;extra
- Antonym: less;fewer
- MemoryTip: 比较级：more + 多音节形容词。

## 43. get

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /ɡet/
- Chinese: 得到；变得；到达
- Collocation: get up;get ready;get to
- Example: How do I get to the railway station?
- 例句: 我怎么去火车站？
- Synonym: receive;become;arrive
- Antonym: lose;give
- MemoryTip: 短语很多：get on / get off / get over。

## 44. who

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.
- IPA (UK): /huː/
- Chinese: 谁；……的人
- Collocation: who is;those who;who else
- Example: Who left this bag on the chair?
- 例句: 谁把包落在椅子上了？
- Synonym: whom;that
- MemoryTip: 主格 who，宾格正式场合用 whom。

## 45. like

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; verb; conj.
- IPA (UK): /laɪk/
- Chinese: 像；喜欢；例如
- Collocation: like this;feel like;would like
- Example: She looks like her mother.
- 例句: 她长得像她母亲。
- Synonym: enjoy;similar to
- Antonym: dislike;unlike
- MemoryTip: 作介词表“像”，作动词表“喜欢”。

## 46. when

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; conj.; pron.
- IPA (UK): /wen/
- Chinese: 什么时候；当……时
- Collocation: when to;by when;since when
- Example: When does the train arrive?
- 例句: 火车什么时候到？
- Synonym: while;whenever
- MemoryTip: 既问时间，也引导时间从句。

## 47. think

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /θɪŋk/
- Chinese: 想；认为；思索
- Collocation: think about;think of;I think
- Example: I think we should leave early.
- 例句: 我认为我们该早点出发。
- Synonym: believe;consider
- MemoryTip: think of=想起；think about=考虑。

## 48. make

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /meɪk/
- Chinese: 做；制造；使
- Collocation: make sure;make a decision;make friends
- Example: She made a cake for the party.
- 例句: 她为派对做了一个蛋糕。
- Synonym: create;produce;cause
- Antonym: destroy;break
- MemoryTip: make sb do = 让某人做某事。

## 49. time

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; verb
- IPA (UK): /taɪm/
- Chinese: 时间；次数；时机
- Collocation: on time;take time;have time
- Example: We do not have much time left.
- 例句: 我们剩下的时间不多了。
- Synonym: moment;occasion;period
- MemoryTip: times 可表倍数或次数。

## 50. see

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /siː/
- Chinese: 看见；理解；见面
- Collocation: see you;see as;I see
- Example: Did you see the notice on the board?
- 例句: 你看到黑板上的通知了吗？
- Synonym: watch;notice;understand
- Antonym: miss;ignore
- MemoryTip: see 无意识看见；watch 有意观看。

## 51. what

- CEFR: A1
- POS: pron.; det.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /wɒt/
- Chinese: 什么；多么
- Collocation: what about;what if;what for
- Example: What is your favourite subject?
- 例句: 你最喜欢的科目是什么？
- Synonym: which;how
- MemoryTip: What a day! 感叹句很常见。

## 52. up

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; prep.; adj.
- IPA (UK): /ʌp/
- Chinese: 向上；起来；完成
- Collocation: get up;wake up;give up
- Example: Please stand up when the teacher comes in.
- 例句: 老师进来时请起立。
- Synonym: upwards;aloft
- Antonym: down
- MemoryTip: 大量动词短语含 up，表完成或上升。

## 53. some

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /sʌm/
- Chinese: 一些；某个；大约
- Collocation: some people;some of;for some time
- Example: Would you like some tea?
- 例句: 你想喝点茶吗？
- Synonym: a few;several
- Antonym: none;all
- MemoryTip: 肯定句多用 some，疑问/否定常改 any。

## 54. other

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.; pron.
- IPA (UK): /ˈʌðə(r)/
- Chinese: 其他的；另一个
- Collocation: each other;the other;other than
- Example: Do you have any other questions?
- 例句: 你还有其他问题吗？
- Synonym: another;different
- Antonym: same
- MemoryTip: the other=两者中另一个；others=其他人/物。

## 55. out

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; prep.; adj.
- IPA (UK): /aʊt/
- Chinese: 出去；外面；熄灭
- Collocation: go out;find out;out of
- Example: She went out for a short walk.
- 例句: 她出去散了一会儿步。
- Synonym: outside;away
- Antonym: in;inside
- MemoryTip: out of = 从……出来 / 用完。

## 56. good

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.; noun
- IPA (UK): /ɡʊd/
- Chinese: 好的；擅长的；好处
- Collocation: good at;good news;for good
- Example: This is a good place for a picnic.
- 例句: 这是一个野餐的好地方。
- Synonym: nice;fine;excellent
- Antonym: bad;poor
- MemoryTip: better / best 是其比较级与最高级。

## 57. people

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /ˈpiːpl/
- Chinese: 人；人们；民族
- Collocation: young people;many people;local people
- Example: Many people use public transport every day.
- 例句: 许多人每天使用公共交通。
- Synonym: persons;folks
- MemoryTip: 通常当复数：people are…。

## 58. year

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /jɪə(r)/
- Chinese: 年；岁；学年
- Collocation: next year;every year;for years
- Example: She spent a year studying abroad.
- 例句: 她在国外学习了一年。
- Synonym: annum;twelve months
- MemoryTip: years old 表示年龄。

## 59. take

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /teɪk/
- Chinese: 拿；带；花费；乘坐
- Collocation: take care;take place;take part
- Example: It takes twenty minutes to walk there.
- 例句: 步行到那里要二十分钟。
- Synonym: bring;carry;accept
- Antonym: give;leave
- MemoryTip: take 强调带走；bring 强调带来。

## 60. no

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; adv.; interj.
- IPA (UK): /nəʊ/
- Chinese: 没有；不；不是的
- Collocation: no longer;no one;no problem
- Example: There is no milk left in the fridge.
- 例句: 冰箱里没有牛奶了。
- Synonym: not any;none
- Antonym: yes;some
- MemoryTip: no + 名词 = not any + 名词。

## 61. well

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; adj.; interj.
- IPA (UK): /wel/
- Chinese: 好地；健康的；嗯
- Collocation: as well;well done;get well
- Example: She speaks English very well.
- 例句: 她英语说得很好。
- Synonym: fine;properly
- Antonym: badly;ill
- MemoryTip: 作形容词常指健康：feel well。

## 62. because

- CEFR: A1
- POS: conj.
- IPA (UK): /bɪˈkɒz/
- Chinese: 因为
- Collocation: because of;just because;because why
- Example: We stayed indoors because it was cold.
- 例句: 因为天冷，我们待在室内。
- Synonym: since;as;for
- Antonym: although
- MemoryTip: because of + 名词短语。

## 63. very

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /ˈveri/
- Chinese: 非常；很
- Collocation: very much;very good;very well
- Example: The film was very interesting.
- 例句: 这部电影非常有趣。
- Synonym: extremely;really
- Antonym: slightly
- MemoryTip: very + 形容词/副词，不可直接修饰动词。

## 64. just

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; adj.
- IPA (UK): /dʒʌst/
- Chinese: 刚刚；只是；公正的
- Collocation: just now;just in time;just as
- Example: I have just finished my homework.
- 例句: 我刚刚做完作业。
- Synonym: only;recently;fair
- Antonym: unfair
- MemoryTip: 完成时里 just 表“刚刚”。

## 65. come

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /kʌm/
- Chinese: 来；到达；出现
- Collocation: come back;come from;come on
- Example: Please come to my office after class.
- 例句: 下课后请到我办公室来。
- Synonym: arrive;approach
- Antonym: go;leave
- MemoryTip: come 朝说话者来；go 离开说话者。

## 66. could

- CEFR: A1
- POS: modal
- IPA (UK): /kʊd/
- Chinese: 能；可以；可能（过去或委婉）
- Collocation: could you;could be;as could
- Example: Could you open the door for me?
- 例句: 你能帮我开一下门吗？
- Synonym: can;might;would
- MemoryTip: 比 can 更礼貌，也表过去能力。

## 67. work

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; verb
- IPA (UK): /wɜːk/
- Chinese: 工作；劳动；起作用
- Collocation: at work;work hard;go to work
- Example: She started work at nine this morning.
- 例句: 她今天早上九点开始工作。
- Synonym: job;labour;function
- Antonym: rest;play
- MemoryTip: 不可数常指劳动；job 多指具体职位。

## 68. use

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /juːz/; /juːs/
- Chinese: 使用；用途
- Collocation: use up;make use of;in use
- Example: May I use your phone for a minute?
- 例句: 我可以用一下你的手机吗？
- Synonym: employ;utilise
- Antonym: waste;ignore
- MemoryTip: 动词读 /juːz/，名词读 /juːs/。

## 69. than

- CEFR: A1
- POS: conj.; prep.
- IPA (UK): /ðæn/
- Chinese: 比
- Collocation: more than;rather than;other than
- Example: This book is longer than that one.
- 例句: 这本书比那本更长。
- Synonym: compared with
- MemoryTip: 比较级后接 than。

## 70. now

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; conj.; noun
- IPA (UK): /naʊ/
- Chinese: 现在；目前
- Collocation: right now;from now on;by now
- Example: We need to leave now or we will be late.
- 例句: 我们现在就得走，否则会迟到。
- Synonym: currently;at present
- Antonym: then;later
- MemoryTip: now and then = 偶尔。

## 71. then

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /ðen/
- Chinese: 然后；那时；那么
- Collocation: and then;since then;by then
- Example: First wash the vegetables, then cook them.
- 例句: 先洗菜，然后烹调。
- Synonym: next;afterwards;at that time
- Antonym: now
- MemoryTip: 既表顺序，也表“那时”。

## 72. also

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /ˈɔːlsəʊ/
- Chinese: 也；而且
- Collocation: not only also;and also;also known as
- Example: She can also speak a little French.
- 例句: 她也会说一点法语。
- Synonym: too;as well;moreover
- MemoryTip: also 多在句中；too 常在句末。

## 73. into

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.
- IPA (UK): /ˈɪntuː/
- Chinese: 进入；变成
- Collocation: go into;turn into;look into
- Example: He walked into the classroom quietly.
- 例句: 他安静地走进教室。
- Synonym: inside;in
- Antonym: out of
- MemoryTip: 强调进入内部：into the room。

## 74. only

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; adj.
- IPA (UK): /ˈəʊnli/
- Chinese: 仅仅；唯一的
- Collocation: not only;only if;the only
- Example: Only three people came to the meeting.
- 例句: 只有三个人来开会。
- Synonym: just;sole;merely
- MemoryTip: 位置不同可能改变句子重点。

## 75. look

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /lʊk/
- Chinese: 看；看起来；外观
- Collocation: look at;look for;look after
- Example: Please look at the board carefully.
- 例句: 请仔细看黑板。
- Synonym: see;watch;appear
- MemoryTip: look at/for/after 搭配义差很大。

## 76. want

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /wɒnt/
- Chinese: 想要；需要
- Collocation: want to;want for;in want of
- Example: I want to learn how to cook.
- 例句: 我想学做饭。
- Synonym: wish;desire;need
- Antonym: reject
- MemoryTip: want sb to do = 想让某人做。

## 77. give

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /ɡɪv/
- Chinese: 给；提供；产生
- Collocation: give up;give back;give a talk
- Example: Could you give me some advice?
- 例句: 你能给我一些建议吗？
- Synonym: offer;provide;hand
- Antonym: take;receive
- MemoryTip: give sb sth 或 give sth to sb。

## 78. first

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; adv.; noun
- IPA (UK): /fɜːst/
- Chinese: 第一；首先；初次
- Collocation: first of all;at first;first time
- Example: First, we need to check the timetable.
- 例句: 首先，我们需要核对时刻表。
- Synonym: initial;primary
- Antonym: last;final
- MemoryTip: at first=起初；first of all=首先。

## 79. new

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.
- IPA (UK): /njuː/
- Chinese: 新的；陌生的
- Collocation: new year;brand new;new to
- Example: They moved into a new flat last week.
- 例句: 他们上周搬进了新公寓。
- Synonym: fresh;modern;recent
- Antonym: old;used
- MemoryTip: new to sth = 对……不熟悉。

## 80. way

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; adv.
- IPA (UK): /weɪ/
- Chinese: 方式；路；方法
- Collocation: by the way;on the way;in this way
- Example: Is this the way to the post office?
- 例句: 这是去邮局的路吗？
- Synonym: method;road;manner
- MemoryTip: way 既指路，也指做事方法。

## 81. find

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /faɪnd/
- Chinese: 找到；发现；觉得
- Collocation: find out;find it hard;find a way
- Example: I cannot find my keys anywhere.
- 例句: 我到处都找不到钥匙。
- Synonym: discover;locate;feel
- Antonym: lose;miss
- MemoryTip: find out = 查明事实。

## 82. over

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; adv.; adj.
- IPA (UK): /ˈəʊvə(r)/
- Chinese: 在……上方；结束；越过
- Collocation: over there;all over;get over
- Example: The meeting will be over by five.
- 例句: 会议五点前会结束。
- Synonym: above;across;finished
- Antonym: under
- MemoryTip: be over = 结束；get over = 克服。

## 83. any

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /ˈeni/
- Chinese: 任何；一些（疑/否）
- Collocation: any more;in any case;any time
- Example: Do you have any questions about the text?
- 例句: 你对课文有任何问题吗？
- Synonym: some;every
- Antonym: none
- MemoryTip: 疑问否定用 any；肯定常用 some。

## 84. after

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; conj.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /ˈɑːftə(r)/
- Chinese: 在……之后
- Collocation: after all;look after;after school
- Example: We went for a walk after dinner.
- 例句: 晚饭后我们去散步了。
- Synonym: following;later
- Antonym: before
- MemoryTip: after all = 毕竟。

## 85. day

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /deɪ/
- Chinese: 天；白天；日子
- Collocation: one day;every day;the other day
- Example: What a beautiful day it is today!
- 例句: 今天天气真好！
- Synonym: date;daytime
- Antonym: night
- MemoryTip: day by day = 一天天。

## 86. where

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; conj.; pron.
- IPA (UK): /weə(r)/
- Chinese: 在哪里；……的地方
- Collocation: where to;anywhere;where from
- Example: Where did you put the tickets?
- 例句: 你把票放哪里了？
- Synonym: wherever
- MemoryTip: 既问地点，也引导地点从句。

## 87. thing

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /θɪŋ/
- Chinese: 东西；事情；情况
- Collocation: for one thing;the thing is;among other things
- Example: I have many things to do this weekend.
- 例句: 这个周末我有很多事要做。
- Synonym: matter;object;stuff
- MemoryTip: 口语里 thing 常泛指事情。

## 88. most

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /məʊst/
- Chinese: 大多数；最
- Collocation: most of;at most;most importantly
- Example: Most students in this class like sports.
- 例句: 这个班大多数学生喜欢运动。
- Synonym: majority;nearly all
- Antonym: least;fewest
- MemoryTip: the most + 形容词 = 最高级。

## 89. should

- CEFR: A1
- POS: modal
- IPA (UK): /ʃʊd/
- Chinese: 应该；理应
- Collocation: should be;should have;why should
- Example: You should drink more water every day.
- 例句: 你应该每天多喝水。
- Synonym: ought to;must
- Antonym: shouldn't
- MemoryTip: should have done = 本该做却未做。

## 90. need

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; modal; noun
- IPA (UK): /niːd/
- Chinese: 需要；必要
- Collocation: need to;in need;need for
- Example: We need more chairs for the meeting.
- 例句: 我们开会需要更多椅子。
- Synonym: require;want;must
- MemoryTip: 实义动词 need to do；情态否定 needn't。

## 91. much

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /mʌtʃ/
- Chinese: 许多（不可数）；很
- Collocation: how much;too much;as much as
- Example: There is not much sugar left.
- 例句: 剩下的糖不多了。
- Synonym: a lot;greatly
- Antonym: little
- MemoryTip: much 修不可数；many 修可数。

## 92. right

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.; adv.; noun
- IPA (UK): /raɪt/
- Chinese: 正确的；右边；权利
- Collocation: all right;right now;the right to
- Example: Turn right at the next traffic lights.
- 例句: 在下一个红绿灯处右转。
- Synonym: correct;proper
- Antonym: wrong;left
- MemoryTip: 既表对错，也表左右与权利。

## 93. how

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; conj.
- IPA (UK): /haʊ/
- Chinese: 如何；怎样；多么
- Collocation: how to;how about;how long
- Example: How can I improve my listening skills?
- 例句: 我怎样才能提高听力？
- Synonym: in what way
- MemoryTip: how + adj./adv. 可表感叹。

## 94. back

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; noun; adj.; verb
- IPA (UK): /bæk/
- Chinese: 回；背部；支持
- Collocation: come back;go back;at the back
- Example: Please put the book back on the shelf.
- 例句: 请把书放回书架上。
- Synonym: behind;return
- Antonym: front;forward
- MemoryTip: back 作动词也可表“支持”。

## 95. mean

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; adj.
- IPA (UK): /miːn/
- Chinese: 意思是；意味着；刻薄的
- Collocation: mean to;what do you mean;by means of
- Example: What does this word mean?
- 例句: 这个词是什么意思？
- Synonym: signify;intend;unkind
- Antonym: kind
- MemoryTip: I mean… 常用来澄清说法。

## 96. even

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; adj.
- IPA (UK): /ˈiːvn/
- Chinese: 甚至；连；平的
- Collocation: even if;even more;even so
- Example: Even a child can understand this rule.
- 例句: 连小孩子都能理解这条规则。
- Synonym: still;yet;flat
- Antonym: odd;uneven
- MemoryTip: even if = 即使。

## 97. may

- CEFR: A1
- POS: modal; noun
- IPA (UK): /meɪ/
- Chinese: 可以；可能；五月
- Collocation: may be;may as well;May Day
- Example: You may leave when you finish the test.
- 例句: 考完试你就可以离开。
- Synonym: might;can;could
- Antonym: must not
- MemoryTip: 表允许或可能性；大写 May 是五月。

## 98. here

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /hɪə(r)/
- Chinese: 这里；在此刻
- Collocation: come here;over here;here and there
- Example: Please sit here next to me.
- 例句: 请坐在我旁边这里。
- Synonym: in this place
- Antonym: there
- MemoryTip: Here you are. = 给你。

## 99. many

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.
- IPA (UK): /ˈmeni/
- Chinese: 许多（可数）
- Collocation: how many;many of;as many as
- Example: Many shops are closed on Sunday.
- 例句: 许多商店周日关门。
- Synonym: lots of;numerous
- Antonym: few
- MemoryTip: many + 复数名词。

## 100. such

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; pron.; prep.
- IPA (UK): /sʌtʃ/
- Chinese: 这样的；如此
- Collocation: such as;such a;as such
- Example: I have never seen such a beautiful sunset.
- 例句: 我从未见过如此美丽的日落。
- Synonym: so;this kind of
- MemoryTip: such as = 例如；such a + 单数名词。

## 101. last

- CEFR: A1
- POS: det.; adv.; verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /lɑːst/
- Chinese: 最后的；上一个；持续；上次
- Collocation: at last;last night;last for
- Example: I saw her last week at the market.
- 例句: 我上周在市场见到了她。
- Synonym: final;previous;endure
- Antonym: first;next
- MemoryTip: at last=终于；last night=昨晚。

## 102. child

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /tʃaɪld/
- Chinese: 孩子；儿童
- Collocation: young child;child care;only child
- Example: The child is learning to ride a bike.
- 例句: 这个孩子正在学习骑自行车。
- Synonym: kid;youngster
- Antonym: adult
- MemoryTip: 复数 children，不规则变化。

## 103. tell

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /tel/
- Chinese: 告诉；讲述；辨别
- Collocation: tell a story;tell the truth;tell from
- Example: Please tell me your phone number.
- 例句: 请告诉我你的电话号码。
- Synonym: say;inform;narrate
- Antonym: conceal
- MemoryTip: tell sb sth；say 一般不直接加间接宾语。

## 104. really

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /ˈrɪəli/
- Chinese: 真正地；确实；非常
- Collocation: really good;not really;really mean
- Example: I really enjoy reading before bed.
- 例句: 我真的很喜欢睡前阅读。
- Synonym: truly;actually;very
- MemoryTip: 可加强语气，也可表惊讶：Really?

## 105. call

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /kɔːl/
- Chinese: 打电话；称呼；呼叫；电话
- Collocation: call for;give a call;call off
- Example: I will call you after the meeting.
- 例句: 会后我会给你打电话。
- Synonym: phone;name;summon
- MemoryTip: call off = 取消。

## 106. before

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; conj.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /bɪˈfɔː(r)/
- Chinese: 在……之前
- Collocation: before long;the day before;before class
- Example: Please wash your hands before dinner.
- 例句: 吃饭前请洗手。
- Synonym: prior to;earlier
- Antonym: after
- MemoryTip: before long = 不久以后。

## 107. company

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /ˈkʌmpəni/
- Chinese: 公司；陪伴
- Collocation: in company;company with;join a company
- Example: She works for a software company.
- 例句: 她在一家软件公司工作。
- Synonym: firm;business;companionship
- MemoryTip: keep sb company = 陪伴某人。

## 108. through

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /θruː/
- Chinese: 穿过；通过；自始至终
- Collocation: go through;through the window;all through
- Example: We walked through the quiet park.
- 例句: 我们穿过了安静的公园。
- Synonym: across;via;throughout
- MemoryTip: get through = 通过/打通电话。

## 109. down

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; prep.; adj.; verb
- IPA (UK): /daʊn/
- Chinese: 向下；沿着；写下
- Collocation: sit down;write down;down the road
- Example: Please write down your email address.
- 例句: 请写下你的电子邮箱地址。
- Synonym: below;downwards
- Antonym: up
- MemoryTip: 大量短语含 down：calm down / break down。

## 110. show

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /ʃəʊ/
- Chinese: 展示；表明；演出
- Collocation: show up;on show;show around
- Example: Can you show me how to use this app?
- 例句: 你能演示一下怎么用这个应用吗？
- Synonym: display;demonstrate;reveal
- Antonym: hide
- MemoryTip: show up = 出现。

## 111. life

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /laɪf/
- Chinese: 生活；生命；人生
- Collocation: real life;daily life;way of life
- Example: She enjoys a simple life in the countryside.
- 例句: 她享受乡村的简单生活。
- Synonym: existence;living
- Antonym: death
- MemoryTip: 复数 lives；lifetime = 一生。

## 112. man

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; verb
- IPA (UK): /mæn/
- Chinese: 男人；人类；配备人员
- Collocation: young man;man of;the best man
- Example: A young man helped us carry the bags.
- 例句: 一位年轻男子帮我们搬了行李。
- Synonym: male;guy;human
- Antonym: woman
- MemoryTip: men 为复数；mankind 表人类（偏旧）。

## 113. change

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /tʃeɪndʒ/
- Chinese: 改变；变化；零钱
- Collocation: change of;change into;for a change
- Example: The weather can change quickly in spring.
- 例句: 春天天气变化很快。
- Synonym: alter;shift;modify
- Antonym: remain;keep
- MemoryTip: small change = 零钱。

## 114. place

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; verb
- IPA (UK): /pleɪs/
- Chinese: 地方；放置；名次
- Collocation: in place;take place;out of place
- Example: This is a good place to meet friends.
- 例句: 这是与朋友见面的好地方。
- Synonym: location;spot;put
- MemoryTip: take place = 发生。

## 115. long

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /lɒŋ/
- Chinese: 长的；长久地
- Collocation: how long;long ago;as long as
- Example: How long does the journey take?
- 例句: 这段路程要多久？
- Synonym: lengthy;extended
- Antonym: short;brief
- MemoryTip: as long as = 只要。

## 116. between

- CEFR: A1
- POS: prep.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /bɪˈtwiːn/
- Chinese: 在……之间（两者）
- Collocation: between you and me;in between;choose between
- Example: The café is between the bank and the library.
- 例句: 咖啡馆在银行和图书馆之间。
- Synonym: among;amid
- MemoryTip: 两者用 between，三者以上多用 among。

## 117. feel

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /fiːl/
- Chinese: 感觉；触摸；情感
- Collocation: feel like;feel free;feel better
- Example: I feel tired after a long day at work.
- 例句: 工作一天后我感觉很累。
- Synonym: sense;experience;believe
- MemoryTip: feel like doing = 想要做。

## 118. too

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /tuː/
- Chinese: 也；太
- Collocation: too much;too many;me too
- Example: The coffee is too hot to drink now.
- 例句: 咖啡现在太烫，没法喝。
- Synonym: also;as well;excessively
- MemoryTip: too…to… = 太……以至于不能。

## 119. still

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; adj.
- IPA (UK): /stɪl/
- Chinese: 仍然；静止的；更加
- Collocation: still life;stand still;better still
- Example: She is still waiting for the reply.
- 例句: 她仍在等待回复。
- Synonym: yet;nevertheless;calm
- Antonym: moving;already
- MemoryTip: 肯定句常用 still，否定完成可用 yet。

## 120. problem

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /ˈprɒbləm/
- Chinese: 问题；难题
- Collocation: solve a problem;no problem;have a problem
- Example: We need to solve this problem quickly.
- 例句: 我们需要尽快解决这个问题。
- Synonym: issue;trouble;difficulty
- Antonym: solution
- MemoryTip: no problem 常作礼貌回应。

## 121. write

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /raɪt/
- Chinese: 写；写信；写作
- Collocation: write down;write to;write about
- Example: Please write your name at the top.
- 例句: 请在上方写下你的名字。
- Synonym: compose;note;record
- Antonym: erase
- MemoryTip: wrote / written 为过去式与过去分词。

## 122. same

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.; pron.; adv.
- IPA (UK): /seɪm/
- Chinese: 相同的；同一的
- Collocation: the same;same as;at the same time
- Example: We arrived at the same time.
- 例句: 我们同时到达。
- Synonym: identical;equal
- Antonym: different;other
- MemoryTip: the same as… = 与……相同。

## 123. lot

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; adv.; pron.
- IPA (UK): /lɒt/
- Chinese: 许多；一批；一块地
- Collocation: a lot of;lots of;a lot
- Example: She spends a lot of time reading.
- 例句: 她花很多时间阅读。
- Synonym: plenty;many;much
- Antonym: little;few
- MemoryTip: a lot of 后接可数或不可数均可。

## 124. great

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.; adv.; noun
- IPA (UK): /ɡreɪt/
- Chinese: 很好的；伟大的；大量的
- Collocation: a great deal;great at;the great

- 例句: 我们在音乐会上玩得很开心。
- Synonym: excellent;wonderful;huge
- Antonym: poor;tiny
- MemoryTip: 口语里 great 常表“真棒”。

## 125. try

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /traɪ/
- Chinese: 尝试；试穿；努力
- Collocation: try to;try on;give it a try
- Example: You should try to speak English every day.
- 例句: 你应该每天试着用英语说话。
- Synonym: attempt;test;endeavour
- Antonym: quit;give up
- MemoryTip: try to do 侧重努力；try doing 侧重尝试。

## 126. leave

- Synonym: depart;abandon;holiday
- Antonym: arrive;stay
- MemoryTip: left 既是过去式，也可表“剩下的”。

- Antonym: neither
- MemoryTip: both…and… = 既……又……。

## 132. little

- Antonym: big;much

## 148. high

- Synonym: tall;elevated;peak

## 150. off

## 159. might

## 171. book

## 172. family

## 173. seem

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb

- Chinese: 似乎；好像

- Example: You seem tired today.
- 例句: 你今天看起来很累。
- Synonym: appear;look;sound
- MemoryTip: It seems that… 很常用。

## 174. let

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /let/
- Chinese: 让；允许；出租
- Collocation: let me;let go;let alone
- Example: Please let me know if you need help.
- 例句: 如果你需要帮助请告诉我。
- Synonym: allow;permit;rent
- Antonym: forbid;prevent
- MemoryTip: let sb do（无 to）；let alone=更不必说。

## 175. again

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /əˈɡen/
- Chinese: 再；又；重新
- Collocation: once again;again and again;over again
- Example: Could you say that again, please?
- 例句: 请你再说一遍好吗？
- Synonym: once more;anew
- MemoryTip: time and again = 一再。

## 176. kind

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; adj.
- IPA (UK): /kaɪnd/
- Chinese: 种类；仁慈的；友好的
- Collocation: kind of;of this kind;be kind
- Example: What kind of music do you like?
- 例句: 你喜欢哪种音乐？
- Synonym: type;sort;gentle
- Antonym: cruel;unkind
- MemoryTip: a kind of… / kind of（口语“有点”）。

- Antonym: never;rarely
- MemoryTip: 频度副词，常放在实义动词前。

## 232. plan

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; verb
- IPA (UK): /plæn/
- Chinese: 计划；打算；规划
- Collocation: plan to;make a plan;according to plan
- Example: We plan to visit the museum tomorrow.
- 例句: 我们计划明天参观博物馆。
- Synonym: scheme;intend;arrange
- MemoryTip: plan to do / plan on doing。

## 233. result

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; verb
- IPA (UK): /rɪˈzʌlt/
- Chinese: 结果；成绩；导致
- Collocation: as a result;result in;result from
- Example: Hard work often brings good results.
- 例句: 努力工作常常带来好结果。
- Synonym: outcome;consequence;effect
- Antonym: cause
- MemoryTip: result in=导致；result from=源于。

## 234. away

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.; adj.
- IPA (UK): /əˈweɪ/
- Chinese: 离开；远离；不在
- Collocation: go away;right away;take away
- Example: He is away on holiday this week.
- 例句: 他这周外出度假了。
- Synonym: off;absent;far
- Antonym: here;near
- MemoryTip: right away = 立刻。

## 235. example

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /ɪɡˈzɑːmpl/
- Chinese: 例子；榜样；范例
- Collocation: for example;set an example;an example of
- Example: Can you give me an example of this rule?
- 例句: 你能举一个关于这条规则的例子吗？
- Synonym: instance;sample;model
- MemoryTip: e.g. = for example。

## 236. happen

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /ˈhæpən/
- Chinese: 发生；碰巧
- Collocation: happen to;what happens;as it happens
- Example: What happened to your phone?
- 例句: 你的手机怎么了？
- Synonym: occur;take place;come about
- MemoryTip: happen to do = 碰巧做。

## 237. offer

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /ˈɒfə(r)/
- Chinese: 提供；提议；报价
- Collocation: offer to;special offer;make an offer
- Example: They offered us a free upgrade.
- 例句: 他们给我们提供了免费升级。
- Synonym: propose;provide;bid
- Antonym: refuse;withdraw
- MemoryTip: offer to help = 主动提出帮忙。

## 238. young

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.; noun
- IPA (UK): /jʌŋ/
- Chinese: 年轻的；幼小的；年轻人
- Collocation: young people;young age;the young
- Example: She looks young for her age.
- 例句: 她看上去比实际年龄年轻。
- Synonym: youthful;junior
- Antonym: old;elderly
- MemoryTip: the young = 年轻人（整体）。

## 239. close

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.; verb; adv.; noun
- IPA (UK): /kləʊs/; /kləʊz/
- Chinese: 近的；关闭；亲密的
- Collocation: close to;close down;come close
- Example: Please close the window; it is cold.
- 例句: 请把窗户关上，天冷。
- Synonym: shut;near;end
- Antonym: open;far
- MemoryTip: 形容词/副词 /kləʊs/；动词 /kləʊz/。

## 240. program

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; verb
- IPA (UK): /ˈprəʊɡræm/
- Chinese: 节目；计划；程序；编程
- Collocation: TV program;program of;computer program
- Example: What is your favourite TV program?
- 例句: 你最喜欢的电视节目是什么？
- Synonym: programme;schedule;software
- MemoryTip: 美式拼写 program 作 lemma 保留；英式常写 programme（除计算机义）。

## 241. lead

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /liːd/; /led/
- Chinese: 引导；领导；铅
- Collocation: lead to;take the lead;in the lead
- Example: This path leads to the main hall.
- 例句: 这条路通向主厅。
- Synonym: guide;head;cause
- Antonym: follow
- MemoryTip: 动词 /liːd/；金属铅读 /led/。

## 242. buy

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb; noun
- IPA (UK): /baɪ/
- Chinese: 买；购买；合算货
- Collocation: buy from;buy out;a good buy
- Example: I need to buy some bread on the way home.
- 例句: 我回家路上需要买些面包。
- Synonym: purchase;get;acquire
- Antonym: sell
- MemoryTip: bought 为过去式与过去分词。

## 243. understand

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /ˌʌndəˈstænd/
- Chinese: 理解；明白；谅解
- Collocation: make oneself understood;fully understand;hard to understand
- Example: Do you understand the question?
- 例句: 你理解这个问题吗？
- Synonym: grasp;comprehend;see
- Antonym: misunderstand
- MemoryTip: understood；get it 更口语。

## 244. thank

- Collocation: thank you;thanks to;thank for
- Example: Thank you for your kind help.
- 例句: 感谢你的好心帮助。
- Synonym: appreciate;grateful
- MemoryTip: thanks to = 多亏。

## 245. far

- Collocation: so far;far from;how far
- Example: How far is it from here to the station?
- 例句: 从这里到车站有多远？
- Synonym: distant;much
- Antonym: near;close
- MemoryTip: so far = 到目前为止。

## 246. today

## 247. hour

- Synonym: sixty minutes;period
- MemoryTip: hour 中 h 不发音。

## 248. student

## 249. face

## 253. less

- Collocation: less than;more or less;less and less

- 例句: 请在汤里少放点盐。
- Synonym: fewer;smaller amount
- Antonym: more
- MemoryTip: less 修不可数；可数用 fewer。

## 254. room

## 255. until

- Chinese: 直到……为止
- Collocation: until now;not until;until then
- Example: Please wait here until I come back.
- 例句: 请在这里等到我回来。
- Synonym: till;up to;before
- MemoryTip: till 更口语；否定里 not until=直到……才。

## 263. person

- Antonym: good;fine

## 270. night

## 271. able

- Synonym: capable;competent
- Antonym: unable;incapable
- MemoryTip: be able to 可带各种时态，补 can 的不足。

## 273. whether

## 275. present

## 278. although

- Collocation: although it;even although
- Example: Although he was tired, he kept working.
- 例句: 虽然他很累，但仍继续工作。
- Synonym: though;even though;while
- MemoryTip: 引导让步从句，不可与 but 同句连用。

## 279. sure

## 284. speak

## 285. within

- POS: prep.; adv.

- Collocation: within days;within reach;within the law
- Example: Please reply within three days.
- 例句: 请在三天内回复。
- Synonym: inside;in;inside of
- Antonym: outside;beyond
- MemoryTip: 表时间或空间范围都常用。

## 286. process

## 287. public

## 288. often

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /ˈɒfn/; /ˈɒftən/
- Chinese: 经常；时常
- Collocation: how often;quite often;as often as
- Example: How often do you exercise each week?
- 例句: 你每周多久锻炼一次？
- Synonym: frequently;regularly
- Antonym: rarely;seldom
- MemoryTip: 频度：always > often > sometimes。

## 289. train

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun; verb
- IPA (UK): /treɪn/
- Chinese: 火车；训练；培养
- Collocation: by train;train for;train station
- Example: I usually take the train to work.
- 例句: 我通常坐火车上班。
- Synonym: coach;educate;instruct
- MemoryTip: 既指火车，也作“训练”动词。

## 290. possible

- CEFR: A1
- POS: adj.
- IPA (UK): /ˈpɒsəbl/
- Chinese: 可能的；可行的
- Collocation: as soon as possible;if possible;make possible
- Example: Is it possible to change the meeting time?
- 例句: 可以改一下会议时间吗？
- Synonym: feasible;likely;potential
- Antonym: impossible
- MemoryTip: possibility 是名词。

## 291. actually

- Chinese: 实际上；竟然
- Collocation: actually speaking;well actually
- Example: I thought it was free; actually it costs five pounds.

- Synonym: really;in fact;truly
- MemoryTip: 常用来纠正对方的误解。

- Synonym: quite;preferably;instead

## 346. force

- Antonym: weakness;persuade

## 401. body

- CEFR: A1
- POS: noun
- IPA (UK): /ˈbɒdi/
- Chinese: 身体；主体；团体
- Collocation: body of;human body;body language
- Example: Regular exercise is good for the body.
- 例句: 规律锻炼对身体有好处。
- Synonym: physique;corpus;group
- Antonym: mind;soul
- MemoryTip: body and mind = 身心。

## 402. require

- CEFR: A1
- POS: verb
- IPA (UK): /rɪˈkwaɪə(r)/
- Chinese: 需要；要求
- Collocation: require to;require that;as required
- Example: This job requires patience and care.
- 例句: 这份工作需要耐心与细心。
- Synonym: need;demand;call for
- Antonym: optional
- MemoryTip: requirement 是名词。

## 457. describe

- CEFR: A1

- Chinese: 描述；形容
- Collocation: describe as;describe to;hard to describe
- Example: Can you describe the man you saw?
- 例句: 你能描述一下你见到的那个人吗？
- Synonym: portray;explain;depict
- MemoryTip: description 是名词。

- Synonym: particularly;notably;above all

- MemoryTip: blood：身体里流动的红色液体。

- Synonym: attract;plea
- Antonym: repel
- MemoryTip: appeal to：对某人有吸引力，或向其提出请求。

- Synonym: cipher;rules
- MemoryTip: code：一串约定好的符号/规则。

- Synonym: beloved;expensive
- Antonym: cheap
- MemoryTip: dear：写信抬头的称呼，也可指贵。

- POS: adv.
- IPA (UK): /ˈtɪpɪkli/
- Chinese: 通常；典型地
- Collocation: typically occur;typically take;typically include
- Example: Lessons typically last about forty-five minutes.
- 例句: 课程通常持续大约四十五分钟。
- Synonym: usually;normally
- Antonym: rarely
- MemoryTip: typical + ly：典型地、通常。

- MemoryTip: universe → universal：适用于全体。
